  }

  // Patch application methods

  async applyPatchToGit(
    upstreamPath: string,
    patchContent: string
  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
    const { writeFileSync, unlinkSync } = await import("fs");
    const { join } = await import("path");

    const patchFile = join(upstreamPath, `.temp-patch-${Date.now()}.diff`);

    try {
      // Write patch to temporary file
      writeFileSync(patchFile, patchContent, "utf-8");

      // Apply patch using git apply
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["git", "apply", patchFile],
        upstreamPath
      );

      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    } finally {
      // Clean up temp file
      try {
        unlinkSync(patchFile);
      } catch {
        // Ignore cleanup errors
      }
    }
  }

  async applyPatchToFossil(
    upstreamPath: string,
    patchContent: string
  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
    const { writeFileSync, unlinkSync } = await import("fs");
    const { join } = await import("path");

    const patchFile = join(upstreamPath, `.temp-patch-${Date.now()}.diff`);

    try {
      // Write patch to temporary file
      writeFileSync(patchFile, patchContent, "utf-8");

      // Apply patch using system patch command
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["patch", "-p0", "-i", patchFile],
        upstreamPath
      );

      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    } finally {
      // Clean up temp file
      try {
        unlinkSync(patchFile);
      } catch {
        // Ignore cleanup errors
      }
    }
  }

  async checkUpstreamStatus(
    upstreamPath: string,
    repoType: "git" | "fossil"
  ): Promise<VCSResult & { isClean: boolean }> {
    if (repoType === "git") {
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["git", "status", "--porcelain"],
        upstreamPath
      );

      const isClean = result.success && (!result.output || result.output.trim() === "");

      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
        isClean,
      };
    } else {
      // Fossil: check for changes
      const result = await this.execCommand(
        ["fossil", "changes"],
        upstreamPath
      );

      const isClean = result.success && (!result.output || result.output.trim() === "");

      return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
        isClean,
      };
    }
  }

  // Patch storage helpers

  async ensureUpstreamPatchesDir(sessionPath: string): Promise<string> {
    const { mkdirSync, existsSync } = await import("fs");
    const { join } = await import("path");

    const patchesDir = join(sessionPath, "upstream-patches");

    if (!existsSync(patchesDir)) {
      mkdirSync(patchesDir, { recursive: true });
    }

    return patchesDir;
  }

  generatePatchFilename(): { diffFile: string; jsonFile: string } {
    const now = new Date();
    const timestamp = now.toISOString()
      .replace(/[:T]/g, "-")
      .replace(/\.\d{3}Z$/, "")
      .replace(/-/g, "-")
      .substring(0, 19); // YYYY-MM-DD-HH-MM-SS

    const baseName = `patch-${timestamp}`;

    return {
      diffFile: `${baseName}.diff`,
      jsonFile: `${baseName}.json`,
    };
  }

  async writePatchFile(
    patchesDir: string,
    filename: string,
    content: string
  ): Promise<void> {
    const { writeFileSync } = await import("fs");
    const { join } = await import("path");

    writeFileSync(join(patchesDir, filename), content, "utf-8");
  }

  async writePatchMetadata(
    patchesDir: string,
    filename: string,
    metadata: {
      generatedAt: string;
      fromCommit: string;
      toCommit: string;
      stats: {
        filesAdded: number;
        filesModified: number;
        filesDeleted: number;
      };
    }
  ): Promise<void> {
    const { writeFileSync } = await import("fs");
    const { join } = await import("path");

    writeFileSync(
      join(patchesDir, filename),
      JSON.stringify(metadata, null, 2),
      "utf-8"
    );
  }

  parsePatchStats(diffOutput: string): {
    filesAdded: number;
    filesModified: number;
    filesDeleted: number;
  } {
    const lines = diffOutput.split("\n");
    const stats = {
      filesAdded: 0,
      filesModified: 0,
      filesDeleted: 0,
    };

    for (const line of lines) {
      const trimmed = line.trim();
      if (trimmed.startsWith("ADDED")) {
        stats.filesAdded++;
      } else if (trimmed.startsWith("DELETED")) {
        stats.filesDeleted++;
      } else if (trimmed.startsWith("Index:") || trimmed.startsWith("---")) {
        // Count modified files from Index lines or --- lines with existing file
        if (trimmed.startsWith("Index:")) {
          // Check next lines to see if it's a modification
          const index = lines.indexOf(line);
          if (index < lines.length - 1) {
            const nextLines = lines.slice(index + 1, index + 4);
            const hasOldFile = nextLines.some(l => l.startsWith("---") && !l.includes("/dev/null"));
            const hasNewFile = nextLines.some(l => l.startsWith("+++") && !l.includes("/dev/null"));
            if (hasOldFile && hasNewFile) {
              stats.filesModified++;
            }
          }
        }
      }
    }

    // If we didn't detect modifications via Index, try another approach
    // Look for --- and +++ pairs that both point to actual files (not /dev/null)
    if (stats.filesModified === 0) {
      for (let i = 0; i < lines.length - 1; i++) {
        if (lines[i].startsWith("---") && !lines[i].includes("/dev/null") &&
            lines[i + 1].startsWith("+++") && !lines[i + 1].includes("/dev/null")) {
          stats.filesModified++;
        }
      }
    }

    return stats;
  }
}

export const vcs = new VCS();
oldString:       return {
        success: result.success,
        output: result.output,
        error: result.error || undefined,
      };
    }
  }
}

+
+  // Patch application methods
+
+  async applyPatchToGit(
+    upstreamPath: string,
+    patchContent: string
+  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
+    const { writeFileSync, unlinkSync } = await import("fs");
+    const { join } = await import("path");
+
+    const patchFile = join(upstreamPath, `.temp-patch-${Date.now()}.diff`);
+
+    try {
+      // Write patch to temporary file
+      writeFileSync(patchFile, patchContent, "utf-8");
+
+      // Apply patch using git apply
+      const result = await this.execCommand(
+        ["git", "apply", patchFile],
+        upstreamPath
+      );
+
+      return {
+        success: result.success,
+        output: result.output,
+        error: result.error || undefined,
+      };
+    } finally {
+      // Clean up temp file
+      try {
+        unlinkSync(patchFile);
+      } catch {
+        // Ignore cleanup errors
+      }
+    }
+  }
+
+  async applyPatchToFossil(
+    upstreamPath: string,
+    patchContent: string
+  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
+    const { writeFileSync, unlinkSync } = await import("fs");
+    const { join } = await import("path");
+
+    const patchFile = join(upstreamPath, `.temp-patch-${Date.now()}.diff`);
+
+    try {
+      // Write patch to temporary file
+      writeFileSync(patchFile, patchContent, "utf-8");
+
+      // Apply patch using system patch command
+      const result = await this.execCommand(
+        ["patch", "-p0", "-i", patchFile],
+        upstreamPath
+      );
+
+      return {
+        success: result.success,
+        output: result.output,
+        error: result.error || undefined,
+      };
+    } finally {
+      // Clean up temp file
+      try {
+        unlinkSync(patchFile);
+      } catch {
+        // Ignore cleanup errors
+      }
+    }
+  }
+
+  async checkUpstreamStatus(
+    upstreamPath: string,
+    repoType: "git" | "fossil"
+  ): Promise<VCSResult & { isClean: boolean }> {
+    if (repoType === "git") {
+      const result = await this.execCommand(
+        ["git", "status", "--porcelain"],
+        upstreamPath
+      );
+
+      const isClean = result.success && (!result.output || result.output.trim() === "");
+
+      return {
+        success: result.success,
+        output: result.output,
+        error: result.error || undefined,
+        isClean,
+      };
+    } else {
+      // Fossil: check for changes
+      const result = await this.execCommand(
+        ["fossil", "changes"],
+        upstreamPath
+      );
+
+      const isClean = result.success && (!result.output || result.output.trim() === "");
+
+      return {
+        success: result.success,
+        output: result.output,
+        error: result.error || undefined,
+        isClean,
+      };
+    }
+  }
+
+  // Patch storage helpers
+
+  async ensureUpstreamPatchesDir(sessionPath: string): Promise<string> {
+    const { mkdirSync, existsSync } = await import("fs");
+    const { join } = await import("path");
+
+    const patchesDir = join(sessionPath, "upstream-patches");
+
+    if (!existsSync(patchesDir)) {
+      mkdirSync(patchesDir, { recursive: true });
+    }
+
+    return patchesDir;
+  }
+
+  generatePatchFilename(): { diffFile: string; jsonFile: string } {
+    const now = new Date();
+    const timestamp = now.toISOString()
+      .replace(/[:T]/g, "-")
+      .replace(/\.\d{3}Z$/, "")
+      .replace(/-/g, "-")
+      .substring(0, 19); // YYYY-MM-DD-HH-MM-SS
+
+    const baseName = `patch-${timestamp}`;
+
+    return {
+      diffFile: `${baseName}.diff`,
+      jsonFile: `${baseName}.json`,
+    };
+  }
+
+  async writePatchFile(
+    patchesDir: string,
+    filename: string,
+    content: string
+  ): Promise<void> {
+    const { writeFileSync } = await import("fs");
+    const { join } = await import("path");
+
+    writeFileSync(join(patchesDir, filename), content, "utf-8");
+  }
+
+  async writePatchMetadata(
+    patchesDir: string,
+    filename: string,
+    metadata: {
+      generatedAt: string;
+      fromCommit: string;
+      toCommit: string;
+      stats: {
+        filesAdded: number;
+        filesModified: number;
+        filesDeleted: number;
+      };
+    }
+  ): Promise<void> {
+    const { writeFileSync } = await import("fs");
+    const { join } = await import("path");
+
+    writeFileSync(
+      join(patchesDir, filename),
+      JSON.stringify(metadata, null, 2),
+      "utf-8"
+    );
+  }
+
+  parsePatchStats(diffOutput: string): {
+    filesAdded: number;
+    filesModified: number;
+    filesDeleted: number;
+  } {
+    const lines = diffOutput.split("\n");
+    const stats = {
+      filesAdded: 0,
+      filesModified: 0,
+      filesDeleted: 0,
+    };
+
+    for (const line of lines) {
+      const trimmed = line.trim();
+      if (trimmed.startsWith("ADDED")) {
+        stats.filesAdded++;
+      } else if (trimmed.startsWith("DELETED")) {
+        stats.filesDeleted++;
+      } else if (trimmed.startsWith("Index:") || trimmed.startsWith("---")) {
+        // Count modified files from Index lines or --- lines with existing file
+        if (trimmed.startsWith("Index:")) {
+          // Check next lines to see if it's a modification
+          const index = lines.indexOf(line);
+          if (index < lines.length - 1) {
+            const nextLines = lines.slice(index + 1, index + 4);
+            const hasOldFile = nextLines.some(l => l.startsWith("---") && !l.includes("/dev/null"));
+            const hasNewFile = nextLines.some(l => l.startsWith("+++") && !l.includes("/dev/null"));
+            if (hasOldFile && hasNewFile) {
+              stats.filesModified++;
+            }
+          }
+        }
+      }
+    }
+
+    // If we didn't detect modifications via Index, try another approach
+    // Look for --- and +++ pairs that both point to actual files (not /dev/null)
+    if (stats.filesModified === 0) {
+      for (let i = 0; i < lines.length - 1; i++) {
+        if (lines[i].startsWith("---") && !lines[i].includes("/dev/null") &&
+            lines[i + 1].startsWith("+++") && !lines[i + 1].includes("/dev/null")) {
+          stats.filesModified++;
+        }
+      }
+    }
+
+    return stats;
+  }

286: 
287:   private deleteDirectoryRecursive(dirPath: string): void {
288:     if (!existsSync(dirPath)) return;
289: 
290:     const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
291:     
292:     for (const entry of entries) {
293:       const entryPath = join(dirPath, entry.name);
294:       if (entry.isDirectory()) {
295:         this.deleteDirectoryRecursive(entryPath);
296:       } else {
297:         unlinkSync(entryPath);
298:       }
299:     }
300: 
301:     rmdirSync(dirPath);
302:   }
303: 
304:   async exists(projectId: string, sessionId: string): Promise<boolean> {
305:     return existsSync(this.getSessionFilePath(projectId, sessionId));
306:   }
307: }
308: 
309: export const sessionRepository = new SessionRepository();

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/commits/service.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-09 02:54:59

newString:     // Step 0.5: Ensure agent-workspace has fossil checkout (for legacy sessions)
    const fossilPath = `${session.upstreamPath}/../repo.fossil`;
    const { existsSync } = await import("fs");
    const { join } = await import("path");
    const fslckoutPath = join(session.agentWorkspacePath, ".fslckout");
    
    if (!existsSync(fslckoutPath)) {
      console.log(`[commit] Initializing fossil checkout in agent-workspace...`);
      const openResult = await vcs.openFossil(fossilPath, session.agentWorkspacePath);
      if (!openResult.success) {
        console.error(`[commit] Failed to initialize checkout: ${openResult.error}`);
        return {
          success: false,
          message: "Failed to initialize fossil checkout",
          error: openResult.error || "Checkout initialization failed",
          step: null,
        };
      }
    }

    // Step 1: Sync agent-workspace with repo.fossil
    console.log(`[commit] Step 1: Syncing agent-workspace with repo.fossil...`);
    const syncResult = await vcs.fossilUp(session.agentWorkspacePath);
    if (!syncResult.success) {
      // Check if it's because checkout doesn't exist
      if (syncResult.error?.includes("not within an open check-out") ||
          syncResult.error?.includes("current directory is not within")) {
        console.log(`[commit] Checkout not initialized, opening fossil repo...`);
        const openResult = await vcs.openFossil(fossilPath, session.agentWorkspacePath);
        if (!openResult.success) {
          return {
            success: false,
            message: "Failed to open fossil checkout",
            error: openResult.error || "fossil open failed",
            step: "sync",
          };
        }
        // Retry fossil up after opening
        const retryResult = await vcs.fossilUp(session.agentWorkspacePath);
        if (!retryResult.success) {
          return {
            success: false,
            message: "Failed to sync with agent",
            error: retryResult.error || "fossil up failed after open",
            step: "sync",
          };
        }
      } else {
        return {
          success: false,
          message: "Failed to sync with agent",
          error: syncResult.error || "fossil up failed",
          step: "sync",
        };
      }
    }

    // Step 2: Check upstream status and determine commits to sync
    console.log(`[commit] Step 2: Checking upstream status...`);
    const statusResult = await vcs.checkUpstreamStatus(session.upstreamPath, repoType);
    if (!statusResult.isClean) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: "Upstream has uncommitted changes",
        error: "Please commit or stash changes in upstream before syncing",
        step: "copy",
      };
    }

    // Determine fromCommit and toCommit
    let fromCommit: string;
    let toCommit: string;

    if (session.lastSyncedCommit) {
      fromCommit = session.lastSyncedCommit;
      console.log(`[commit] Using lastSyncedCommit as fromCommit: ${fromCommit.slice(0, 8)}`);
    } else {
      // First sync - get the first commit
      const firstCommitResult = await vcs.getFirstCommit(session.agentWorkspacePath);
      if (!firstCommitResult.success || !firstCommitResult.output) {
        return {
          success: false,
          message: "Failed to get first commit",
          error: firstCommitResult.error || "Could not determine first commit",
          step: "copy",
        };
      }
      fromCommit = firstCommitResult.output.trim();
      console.log(`[commit] Using first commit as fromCommit: ${fromCommit.slice(0, 8)}`);
    }

    // Get current commit
    const currentCommitResult = await vcs.getCurrentCommit(session.agentWorkspacePath);
    if (!currentCommitResult.success || !currentCommitResult.output) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: "Failed to get current commit",
        error: currentCommitResult.error || "Could not determine current commit",
        step: "copy",
      };
    }
    toCommit = currentCommitResult.output.trim();
    console.log(`[commit] Current commit (toCommit): ${toCommit.slice(0, 8)}`);

    // Skip if no changes
    if (fromCommit === toCommit) {
      console.log(`[commit] No new commits to sync`);
      return {
        success: true,
        message: "No changes to commit",
        step: null,
      };
    }

    // Step 3: Generate patch
    console.log(`[commit] Step 3: Generating patch from ${fromCommit.slice(0, 8)} to ${toCommit.slice(0, 8)}...`);
    const patchResult = await vcs.generatePatch(session.agentWorkspacePath, fromCommit, toCommit);
    if (!patchResult.success) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: "Failed to generate patch",
        error: patchResult.error || "Patch generation failed",
        step: "copy",
      };
    }

    if (!patchResult.output || patchResult.output.trim() === "") {
      console.log(`[commit] Patch is empty - no changes to sync`);
      return {
        success: true,
        message: "No changes to commit",
        step: null,
      };
    }

    // Step 4: Store patch in upstream-patches folder
    console.log(`[commit] Step 4: Storing patch in upstream-patches folder...`);
    const sessionPath = `${session.upstreamPath}/..`;
    const patchesDir = await vcs.ensureUpstreamPatchesDir(sessionPath);
    const { diffFile, jsonFile } = vcs.generatePatchFilename();
    
    await vcs.writePatchFile(patchesDir, diffFile, patchResult.output);
    
    // Generate metadata
    const stats = vcs.parsePatchStats(patchResult.output);
    await vcs.writePatchMetadata(patchesDir, jsonFile, {
      generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      fromCommit,
      toCommit,
      stats,
    });
    
    console.log(`[commit] Patch stored: ${diffFile}`);
    console.log(`[commit] Files added: ${stats.filesAdded}, modified: ${stats.filesModified}, deleted: ${stats.filesDeleted}`);

    // Step 5: Apply patch to upstream
    console.log(`[commit] Step 5: Applying patch to upstream...`);
    let applyResult;
    if (repoType === "git") {
      applyResult = await vcs.applyPatchToGit(session.upstreamPath, patchResult.output);
    } else {
      applyResult = await vcs.applyPatchToFossil(session.upstreamPath, patchResult.output);
    }

    if (!applyResult.success) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: "Failed to apply patch to upstream",
        error: applyResult.error || "Patch application failed",
        step: "copy",
      };
    }

    // Step 6: Update lastSyncedCommit
    console.log(`[commit] Step 6: Updating lastSyncedCommit...`);
    await sessionRepository.updateLastSyncedCommit(sessionId, toCommit);

+      console.log(`[commit] Using lastSyncedCommit as fromCommit: ${fromCommit.slice(0, 8)}`);
+    } else {
+      // First sync - get the first commit
+      const firstCommitResult = await vcs.getFirstCommit(session.agentWorkspacePath);
+      if (!firstCommitResult.success || !firstCommitResult.output) {
+        return {
+          success: false,
+          message: "Failed to get first commit",
+          error: firstCommitResult.error || "Could not determine first commit",
+          step: "copy",
+        };
+      }
+      fromCommit = firstCommitResult.output.trim();
+      console.log(`[commit] Using first commit as fromCommit: ${fromCommit.slice(0, 8)}`);
+    }
+
+    // Get current commit
+    const currentCommitResult = await vcs.getCurrentCommit(session.agentWorkspacePath);
+    if (!currentCommitResult.success || !currentCommitResult.output) {
+      return {
+        success: false,
+        message: "Failed to get current commit",
+        error: currentCommitResult.error || "Could not determine current commit",
+        step: "copy",
+      };
+    }
+    toCommit = currentCommitResult.output.trim();
+    console.log(`[commit] Current commit (toCommit): ${toCommit.slice(0, 8)}`);
+
+    // Skip if no changes
+    if (fromCommit === toCommit) {
+      console.log(`[commit] No new commits to sync`);
+      return {
+        success: true,
+        message: "No changes to commit",
+        step: null,
+      };
+    }
+
+    // Step 3: Generate patch
+    console.log(`[commit] Step 3: Generating patch from ${fromCommit.slice(0, 8)} to ${toCommit.slice(0, 8)}...`);
+    const patchResult = await vcs.generatePatch(session.agentWorkspacePath, fromCommit, toCommit);
+    if (!patchResult.success) {
+      return {
+        success: false,
+        message: "Failed to generate patch",
+        error: patchResult.error || "Patch generation failed",
+        step: "copy",
+      };
+    }
+
+    if (!patchResult.output || patchResult.output.trim() === "") {
+      console.log(`[commit] Patch is empty - no changes to sync`);
+      return {
+        success: true,
+        message: "No changes to commit",
+        step: null,
+      };
+    }
+
+    // Step 4: Store patch in upstream-patches folder
+    console.log(`[commit] Step 4: Storing patch in upstream-patches folder...`);
+    const sessionPath = `${session.upstreamPath}/..`;
+    const patchesDir = await vcs.ensureUpstreamPatchesDir(sessionPath);
+    const { diffFile, jsonFile } = vcs.generatePatchFilename();
+    
+    await vcs.writePatchFile(patchesDir, diffFile, patchResult.output);
+    
+    // Generate metadata
+    const stats = vcs.parsePatchStats(patchResult.output);
+    await vcs.writePatchMetadata(patchesDir, jsonFile, {
+      generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
+      fromCommit,
+      toCommit,
+      stats,
+    });
+    
+    console.log(`[commit] Patch stored: ${diffFile}`);
+    console.log(`[commit] Files added: ${stats.filesAdded}, modified: ${stats.filesModified}, deleted: ${stats.filesDeleted}`);
+
+    // Step 5: Apply patch to upstream
+    console.log(`[commit] Step 5: Applying patch to upstream...`);
+    let applyResult;
+    if (repoType === "git") {
+      applyResult = await vcs.applyPatchToGit(session.upstreamPath, patchResult.output);
+    } else {
+      applyResult = await vcs.applyPatchToFossil(session.upstreamPath, patchResult.output);
+    }
+
+    if (!applyResult.success) {
+      return {
+        success: false,
+        message: "Failed to apply patch to upstream",
+        error: applyResult.error || "Patch application failed",
+        step: "copy",
+      };
+    }
+
+    // Step 6: Update lastSyncedCommit
+    console.log(`[commit] Step 6: Updating lastSyncedCommit...`);
+    await sessionRepository.updateLastSyncedCommit(sessionId, toCommit);
\ No newline at end of file
```

866:       // These are the files tracked in the current checkout

868:       const fossilLsResult = await this.execCommand(["fossil", "ls"], agentWorkspacePath);
869:       if (fossilLsResult.success && fossilLsResult.output) {
870:         const lines = fossilLsResult.output.split("\n").filter(line => line.trim());
871:         for (const line of lines) {
872:           fossilTrackedFiles.add(line.trim());
873:         }
874:       }
875: 
876:       // Step 2: Get list of tracked files in upstream (source of truth for deletions)
877:       const upstreamTrackedFiles: string[] = [];
878:       if (fsExistsSync(upstreamPath)) {
879:         const gitLsResult = await this.execCommand(["git", "ls-files"], upstreamPath);
880:         if (gitLsResult.success && gitLsResult.output) {
881:           const lines = gitLsResult.output.split("\n").filter(line => line.trim());

887:       // Exclude VCS metadata directories
888:       // Files on disk but NOT in fossil ls are either:
889:       // - Untracked files (should be copied)
890:       // - Deleted tracked files (should NOT be copied)
891:       const excludeItems = new Set([".git", ".fossil", ".fslckout"]);
892:       
893:       const copyRecursive = (source: string, dest: string, basePath: string = source) => {
894:         if (!fsExistsSync(source)) return;
895: 
896:         const entries = readdirSync(source, { withFileTypes: true });
897:         for (const entry of entries) {
898:           // Skip VCS metadata directories
899:           if (excludeItems.has(entry.name)) continue;

901:           const sourcePath = join(source, entry.name);
902:           const destPath = join(dest, entry.name);
903:           const relativePath = relative(basePath, sourcePath);
904: 
905:           if (entry.isDirectory()) {
906:             if (!fsExistsSync(destPath)) {
907:               mkdirSync(destPath, { recursive: true });

911:             // Only copy if file should exist according to fossil,
912:             // OR if it's not tracked at all (new untracked file)
913:             const shouldCopy = fossilTrackedFiles.has(relativePath) || !upstreamTrackedFiles.includes(relativePath);
914:             if (shouldCopy) {
915:               copyFileSync(sourcePath, destPath);
916:             }
917:           }

### Tool Call [completed]: packages/mimo-platform/src/vcs/index.ts

**Tool:** edit
**Timestamp:** 2026-04-09 02:59:13
**Parameters:**
filePath: /home/bit4bit/src/mimo/packages/mimo-platform/src/vcs/index.ts
oldString:     return {

  async cleanCopyToUpstream(
    agentWorkspacePath: string,
    upstreamPath: string
  ): Promise<VCSResult> {
    const { readdirSync, statSync, copyFileSync, mkdirSync, unlinkSync, rmdirSync } = await import("fs");
    const { join, relative } = await import("path");

    const { existsSync: fsExistsSync } = await import("fs");
    
    try {
      // Step 1: Get list of files that SHOULD exist according to fossil
      // These are the files tracked in the current checkout
      const fossilTrackedFiles: Set<string> = new Set();
      const fossilLsResult = await this.execCommand(["fossil", "ls"], agentWorkspacePath);
      if (fossilLsResult.success && fossilLsResult.output) {
        const lines = fossilLsResult.output.split("\n").filter(line => line.trim());
        for (const line of lines) {
          fossilTrackedFiles.add(line.trim());
        }
      }

      // Step 2: Get list of tracked files in upstream (source of truth for deletions)
      const upstreamTrackedFiles: string[] = [];
      if (fsExistsSync(upstreamPath)) {
        const gitLsResult = await this.execCommand(["git", "ls-files"], upstreamPath);
        if (gitLsResult.success && gitLsResult.output) {
          const lines = gitLsResult.output.split("\n").filter(line => line.trim());
          upstreamTrackedFiles.push(...lines);
        }
      }

      // Step 3: Copy all files from agent-workspace to upstream
      // Exclude VCS metadata directories
      // Files on disk but NOT in fossil ls are either:
      // - Untracked files (should be copied)
      // - Deleted tracked files (should NOT be copied)
      const excludeItems = new Set([".git", ".fossil", ".fslckout"]);
      
      const copyRecursive = (source: string, dest: string, basePath: string = source) => {
        if (!fsExistsSync(source)) return;

        const entries = readdirSync(source, { withFileTypes: true });
        for (const entry of entries) {
          // Skip VCS metadata directories
          if (excludeItems.has(entry.name)) continue;

          const sourcePath = join(source, entry.name);
          const destPath = join(dest, entry.name);
          const relativePath = relative(basePath, sourcePath);

          if (entry.isDirectory()) {
            if (!fsExistsSync(destPath)) {
              mkdirSync(destPath, { recursive: true });
            }
            copyRecursive(sourcePath, destPath, basePath);
          } else {
            // Only copy if file should exist according to fossil,
            // OR if it's not tracked at all (new untracked file)
            const shouldCopy = fossilTrackedFiles.has(relativePath) || !upstreamTrackedFiles.includes(relativePath);
            if (shouldCopy) {
              copyFileSync(sourcePath, destPath);
            }
          }
        }
      };

      if (fsExistsSync(agentWorkspacePath)) {
        copyRecursive(agentWorkspacePath, upstreamPath, agentWorkspacePath);
      }

      // Step 4: Delete from upstream files that are:
      // - Tracked in upstream (from git ls-files)
      // - Either not on agent disk OR not tracked by fossil (meaning deleted)
      for (const trackedFile of upstreamTrackedFiles) {
        const agentFilePath = join(agentWorkspacePath, trackedFile);
        const upstreamFilePath = join(upstreamPath, trackedFile);
        
        // Delete if tracked in upstream but either:
        // 1. Not present on agent disk, OR
        // 2. Present on disk but NOT tracked by fossil (was deleted via fossil rm)
        const existsOnDisk = fsExistsSync(agentFilePath);
        const trackedByFossil = fossilTrackedFiles.has(trackedFile);
        const shouldDelete = !existsOnDisk || !trackedByFossil;
        
        if (shouldDelete && fsExistsSync(upstreamFilePath)) {
          unlinkSync(upstreamFilePath);
          
          // Clean up empty parent directories
          let parentDir = join(upstreamPath, trackedFile);
          while (true) {
            parentDir = join(parentDir, "..");
            const resolvedParent = join(parentDir); // Normalize
            if (resolvedParent === upstreamPath) break;
            
            try {
              const entries = readdirSync(resolvedParent);
              if (entries.length === 0) {
                rmdirSync(resolvedParent);
              } else {
                break;
              }
            } catch {
              break;
            }
          }
        }
      }

      return {
        success: true,
        output: "Files copied successfully",
      };
    } catch (error) {
      return {
        success: false,
        error: `Failed to copy files: ${error}`,
      };
    }
  }

  async commitUpstream(
newString:     return {
      success: false,
      error: result.error || "Failed to get first commit",
    };
  }

  async commitUpstream(
